***nou.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:nou.html>nou</a> (96)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_5">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:nou.html>nou</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:a.html>a</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:variant.html>variant</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:nu.html>nu</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*<a href = vnd.unilang:nu.html>nu</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*<a href = vnd.unilang:nu.html>nu</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb_2"><a href = vnd.unilang:adverb.html>Adverb</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***nummerbord.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:nummerbord.html>nummerbord</a> (14214)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compound <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:nummer.html>nummer</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bord.html>bord</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun"><a href = vnd.unilang:noun.html>Noun</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
